  2035. # [18:14] <mwargers> ok
  2036. # [18:14] <bholley> mwargers: the JS engine has an error handling convention
  2037. # [18:14] * Joins: bjacob (bjacob@13F2CEC5.7672369.D8E68FF6.IP)
  2038. # [18:14] <bholley> mwargers: when code hits an error, it sets a pending exception, and returns false
  2039. # [18:14] <bholley> callers propagate the false value upwards
  2040. # [18:14] <bholley> when it gets to the top, we check if there's a pending exception. If not, we assume it's because we ran out of memory
  2041. # [18:14] <mwargers> ah, I see
  2042. # [18:15] <bholley> mwargers: but if there was a bug somewhere and somebody returned false for some other reason without setting an exception, we'll claim OOM when it was actually something else
  2043. # [18:15] <bholley> mwargers: I don't know if that applies in this case or not
